name:Xâ€iâ€xâ€iâ€râ€aâ€nâ€gâ€râ€aâ€nâ€gâ€yâ€uâ€eâ€câ€aâ€nâ€gâ€qâ€iâ€oâ€nâ€g

posted:Posted May 13, 2024
msg:I haven't written a review for a long time, but this time it's really a pity.
First of all, I booked an oxygen-enriched twin bed. In fact, it doesn't matter whether it has oxygen or not. The main thing is to find the price-performance ratio. After booking, I applied for an upgrade to a higher floor through Ctrip and directly contacted the hotel, but both were rejected because the room type only has the 6th floor. The hotel even said directly that you booked a low-priced room. If you want to live in a good room, you can cancel and book a view room... Of course, as I often travel on business, it is common to ask for an upgrade. It is indeed not 100% satisfied, but more because the hotel is full. Like the previous answer, this is the first time I have encountered it, not to mention that the five-star hotel adheres to the service concept of No excuse. So for the guest room, you can take a look at the real situation of this room type. The overall facilities and equipment of the hotel are simply unsightly. Oh, by the way, the next day I found that the toilet was too old and could not be flushed normally. I repaired it in the morning and the toilet was still the same when I came back at noon.
Secondly, regarding the hotel's supporting services, when checking in, I asked the front desk staff whether the group purchase package on Dianping could be delivered to the room for dining. I was transferred to the catering depar**ent and was told that a 30% service fee would be added for delivery. My God, this is the ceiling of the service fee I have heard in China. I was finally exempted from the high service fee by packing up, but they forgot to give me fruit.
Finally, I had to scan the code when checking out. After scanning, I still couldn't get out. I negotiated with the front desk and was told that a QR code can only be scanned once. The pile of paper disposable parking QR codes at the front desk are inconvenient and not environmentally friendly. I really don't know if the level of Delong hotels is like this?
The only thing that is worth comforting is that a girl named Wang in the Xishi Kitchen of the catering depar**ent, who may just be an intern, helped to ask questions and solve problems.

It is quite convenient to order takeout near the hotel.

msg:I was attending a wedding banquet in Zhuji, and it was too late to return to Jiangsu. My friend recommended Kaiyuan. I didn't expect to be pleasantly surprised. As an old five-star hotel, although the facilities are not as good as those of new hotels, the service and hygiene are outstanding. The room is clean and tidy, and welcome fruit is also given. When the front desk learned that there were children, they immediately sent breakfast for free. The staff of the entire hotel were polite and enthusiastic without making people feel abrupt. The breakfast was also rich, and the staff would follow up in time and patiently ask about your requirements. In short, this stay made people feel very satisfied. Kaiyuan is the king of cost-effectiveness at this price.
